</pre>{% endraw %}Now the time to reverse a list is linear in the length of the list.

## Map {#Map}

Map applies a function to every element of a list to generate a corresponding list.
Map is an example of a _higher-order function_, one which takes a function as an
argument or returns a function as a result:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="map"></a><a id="12867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#12867" class="Function">map</a> <a id="12871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12873" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12875" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12876" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12876" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12878" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12878" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="12880" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12882" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="12885" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12887" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12890" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12876" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12892" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12894" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12878" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12895" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12897" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12899" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="12904" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12876" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12906" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12908" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="12913" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12878" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="12915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#12867" class="Function">map</a> <a id="12919" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12919" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12921" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>        <a id="12931" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="12934" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
<a id="12937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#12867" class="Function">map</a> <a id="12941" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12941" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12944" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12944" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12946" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="12948" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12948" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="12950" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="12953" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="12956" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12941" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12958" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12944" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12960" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="12962" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12867" class="Function">map</a> <a id="12966" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12941" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12968" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12948" class="Bound">xs</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Map of the empty list is the empty list.
Map of a non-empty list yields a list
with head the same as the function applied to the head of the given list,
and tail the same as map of the function applied to the tail of the given list.

Here is an example showing how to use map to increment every element of a list:

It is often convenient to exploit currying by applying
map to a function to yield a new function, and at a later
point applying the resulting function:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="sucs"></a><a id="13782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#13782" class="Function">sucs</a> <a id="13787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13789" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="13794" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="13796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13798" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="13803" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

  <a id="13953" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Any type that is parameterised on another type, such as lists, has a
corresponding map, which accepts a function and returns a function
from the type parameterised on the domain of the function to the type
parameterised on the range of the function. Further, a type that is
parameterised on _n_ types will have a map that is parameterised on
_n_ functions.


#### Exercise `map-compose` (practice)

Prove that the map of a composition is equal to the composition of two maps:

    map (g ∘ f) ≡ map g ∘ map f

The last step of the proof requires extensionality.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="14527" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `map-++-distribute` (practice)

Prove the following relationship between map and append:

    map f (xs ++ ys) ≡ map f xs ++ map f ys

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="14708" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>

#### Exercise `map-Tree` (practice)

Define a type of trees with leaves of type `A` and internal

  <a id="Tree.leaf"></a><a id="14892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#14892" class="InductiveConstructor">leaf</a> <a id="14897" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14899" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#14867" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14901" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14903" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#14861" class="Datatype">Tree</a> <a id="14908" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#14867" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14910" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#14869" class="Bound">B</a>

## Fold {#Fold}

Fold takes an operator and a value, and uses the operator to combine
each of the elements of the list, taking the given value as the result
for the empty list:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="foldr"></a><a id="15293" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15299" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15301" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15303" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15304" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15304" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15306" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15306" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15308" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15310" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="15313" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15317" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15318" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15304" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15320" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15322" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15306" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15326" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15306" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15327" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15329" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15331" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15306" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15335" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="15340" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15304" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15342" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15344" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15306" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="15346" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15352" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15352" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15356" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15356" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15358" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>        <a id="15368" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15371" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15356" class="Bound">e</a>
<a id="15373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15379" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15379" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15383" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15383" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15386" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15386" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15388" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15390" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15390" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="15392" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="15395" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15398" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15386" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15400" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15379" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="15402" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15408" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15379" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15412" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15383" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15414" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15390" class="Bound">xs</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Fold of the empty list is the given value.
Fold of a non-empty list uses the operator to combine
the head of the list and the fold of the tail of the list.

Here is an example showing how to use fold to find the sum of a list:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="15652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15652" class="Function">_</a> <a id="15654" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15656" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15662" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="15666" class="Number">0</a> <a id="15668" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="15670" class="Number">1</a> <a id="15672" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15674" class="Number">2</a> <a id="15676" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15678" class="Number">3</a> <a id="15680" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15682" class="Number">4</a> <a id="15684" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="15686" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="15688" class="Number">10</a>
<a id="15691" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15693" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="15697" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2597" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="15707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15713" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="15717" class="Number">0</a> <a id="15719" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15720" class="Number">1</a> <a id="15722" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15724" class="Number">2</a> <a id="15726" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15728" class="Number">3</a> <a id="15730" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15732" class="Number">4</a> <a id="15734" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15736" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a><a id="15738" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15877" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="15885" class="Number">1</a> <a id="15887" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15890" class="Number">2</a> <a id="15892" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15895" class="Number">3</a> <a id="15897" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15899" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15900" class="Number">4</a> <a id="15902" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15910" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="15914" class="Number">0</a> <a id="15916" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a><a id="15918" class="Symbol">)))</a>
  <a id="15924" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="15932" class="Number">1</a> <a id="15934" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15936" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15937" class="Number">2</a> <a id="15939" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15941" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15942" class="Number">3</a> <a id="15944" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15946" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15947" class="Number">4</a> <a id="15949" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="15951" class="Number">0</a><a id="15952" class="Symbol">)))</a>
  <a id="15958" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Here we have an instance of `foldr` where `A` and `B` are both `ℕ`.
Fold requires time linear in the length of the list.

It is often convenient to exploit currying by applying
fold to an operator and a value to yield a new function,
and at a later point applying the resulting function:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="sum"></a><a id="16256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16256" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16260" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16262" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="16267" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="16269" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16271" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
<a id="16273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16256" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16277" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16279" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="16285" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="16289" class="Number">0</a>

<a id="16292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16292" class="Function">_</a> <a id="16294" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16296" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#16256" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16300" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16302" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16304" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16306" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16308" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16310" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16312" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16314" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16316" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="16318" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16320" class="Number">10</a>
<a id="16323" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="16325" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16329" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2597" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="16339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16256" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16343" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16345" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16347" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16349" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16351" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16353" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16355" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16357" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16359" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="16363" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="16377" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="16381" class="Number">0</a> <a id="16383" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16385" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16387" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16389" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16391" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16393" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16395" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16397" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16399" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="16403" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16411" class="Number">10</a>
  <a id="16416" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Just as the list type has two constructors, `[]` and `_∷_`,
so the fold function takes two arguments, `e` and `_⊗_`
(in addition to the list argument).
In general, a data type with _n_ constructors will have
a corresponding fold function that takes _n_ arguments.

As another example, observe that

    foldr _∷_ [] xs ≡ xs

Here, if `xs` is of type `List A`, then we see we have an instance of
`foldr` where `A` is `A` and `B` is `List A`.  It follows that

    xs ++ ys ≡ foldr _∷_ ys xs

Demonstrating both these equations is left as an exercise.


#### Exercise `product` (recommended)

Use fold to define a function to find the product of a list of numbers.
For example:

    product [ 1 , 2 , 3 , 4 ] ≡ 24

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17140" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `foldr-++` (recommended)

Show that fold and append are related as follows:

    foldr _⊗_ e (xs ++ ys) ≡ foldr _⊗_ (foldr _⊗_ e ys) xs

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17323" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `foldr-∷` (practice)

Show

    foldr _∷_ [] xs ≡ xs

Show as a consequence of `foldr-++` above that

    xs ++ ys ≡ foldr _∷_ ys xs    


{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17508" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `map-is-foldr` (practice)

Show that map can be defined using fold:

    map f ≡ foldr (λ x xs → f x ∷ xs) []

The proof requires extensionality.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17701" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `fold-Tree` (practice)

Define a suitable fold function for the type of trees given earlier:

    fold-Tree : ∀ {A B C : Set} → (A → C) → (C → B → C → C) → Tree A B → C


{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17918" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `map-is-fold-Tree` (practice)

Demonstrate an analogue of `map-is-foldr` for the type of trees.

#### Exercise `sum-downFrom` (stretch)

Define a function that counts down as follows:

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="18283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Function">_</a> <a id="18285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18287" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18180" class="Function">downFrom</a> <a id="18296" class="Number">3</a> <a id="18298" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18300" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="18302" class="Number">2</a> <a id="18304" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18306" class="Number">1</a> <a id="18308" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18310" class="Number">0</a> <a id="18312" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}Prove that the sum of the numbers `(n - 1) + ⋯ + 0` is
equal to `n * (n ∸ 1) / 2`:

    sum (downFrom n) * 2 ≡ n * (n ∸ 1)


## Monoids

Typically when we use a fold the operator is associative and the
value is a left and right identity for the operator, meaning that the
operator and the value form a _monoid_.

We can define a monoid as a suitable record type:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="18694" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="IsMonoid"></a><a id="18701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18701" class="Record">IsMonoid</a> <a id="18710" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18711" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18713" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18715" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18718" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18721" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="18725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18727" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18729" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18731" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18733" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18735" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18736" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18739" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18739" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="18741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18743" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18744" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18746" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18748" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="18752" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="18760" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="IsMonoid.assoc"></a><a id="18770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18770" class="Field">assoc</a> <a id="18776" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18778" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18781" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18781" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18783" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18783" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18785" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18785" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18789" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18790" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18792" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18794" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18795" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18781" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18797" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="18799" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18783" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18800" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18802" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="18804" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18785" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18806" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18808" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18781" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18810" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="18812" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18813" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18783" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18815" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="18817" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18785" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18818" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="IsMonoid.identityˡ"></a><a id="18824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18824" class="Field">identityˡ</a> <a id="18834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18836" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18839" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18839" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18841" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18843" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18711" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18844" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18846" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18848" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18739" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="18850" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18721" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="18852" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18839" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18854" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18856" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18839" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="18897" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="18902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18701" class="Module">IsMonoid</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
As examples, sum and zero, multiplication and one, and append and the empty
list, are all examples of monoids:

If `_⊗_` and `e` form a monoid, then we can re-express fold on the
same operator and an arbitrary value:

In a previous exercise we showed the following.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="20230" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="foldr-++"></a><a id="20242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20242" class="Postulate">foldr-++</a> <a id="20251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20253" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20255" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20256" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20258" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20260" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="20263" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20265" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20266" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20266" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20272" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20274" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20276" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20280" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20281" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20283" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20284" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20284" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20286" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20288" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20289" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20292" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20292" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="20295" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20295" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="20298" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20300" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="20305" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20256" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20306" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20308" class="Symbol">→</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
As a consequence, using a previous exercise, we have the following:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="foldr-monoid-++"></a><a id="20447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20447" class="Function">foldr-monoid-++</a> <a id="20463" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20465" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20467" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20468" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20472" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="20475" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20478" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20484" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20486" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20488" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20492" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20493" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20495" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20496" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20496" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20498" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20500" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20501" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20503" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20505" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#18701" class="Record">IsMonoid</a> <a id="20514" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20518" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20496" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20520" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="20524" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20527" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="20530" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20530" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="20533" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20535" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="20540" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20468" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20541" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20545" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="20551" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20555" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20496" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20558" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20527" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="20561" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#3467" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="20564" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20530" class="Bound">ys</a><a id="20566" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20568" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="20570" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="20576" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20580" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20496" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20582" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20527" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="20585" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="20587" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="20593" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20478" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20597" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20496" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20599" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#20530" class="Bound">ys</a>

#### Exercise `foldl` (practice)

Define a function `foldl` which is analogous to `foldr`, but where
operations associate to the left rather than the right.  For example:

    foldr _⊗_ e [ x , y , z ]  =  x ⊗ (y ⊗ (z ⊗ e))
    foldl _⊗_ e [ x , y , z ]  =  ((e ⊗ x) ⊗ y) ⊗ z

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="21119" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

#### Exercise `foldr-monoid-foldl` (practice)

Show that if `_⊗_` and `e` form a monoid, then `foldr _⊗_ e` and
`foldl _⊗_ e` always compute the same result.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="21311" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

## All {#All}

We can also define predicates over lists. Two of the most important
are `All` and `Any`.

Predicate `All P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by every element of a list:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="21531" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="All"></a><a id="21536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21540" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21541" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21541" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21543" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21545" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="21548" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21550" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21551" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21555" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21541" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21557" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21559" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="21562" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21566" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="21571" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21541" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21573" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21575" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="21579" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="All.[]"></a><a id="21587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21587" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>  <a id="21591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21593" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21597" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21599" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
  <a id="All._∷_"></a><a id="21604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_∷_</a> <a id="21608" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21610" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21612" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21613" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21613" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21617" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21541" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21618" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21620" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21621" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21621" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="21624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21626" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="21631" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21541" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21632" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21634" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21636" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21638" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21613" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21640" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21642" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21646" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21648" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21621" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="21651" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21653" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21657" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21660" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21613" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21662" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="21664" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21621" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="21666" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The type has two constructors, reusing the names of the same constructors for lists.
The first asserts that `P` holds for every element of the empty list.
The second asserts that if `P` holds of the head of a list and for every
element of the tail of a list, then `P` holds for every element of the list.
Agda uses types to disambiguate whether the constructor is building
a list or evidence that `All P` holds.

For example, `All (_≤ 2)` holds of a list where every element is less
than or equal to two.  Recall that `z≤n` proves `zero ≤ n` for any
`n`, and that if `m≤n` proves `m ≤ n` then `s≤s m≤n` proves `suc m ≤
suc n`, for any `m` and `n`:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="22324" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22324" class="Function">_</a> <a id="22326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22328" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="22332" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22333" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#895" class="Datatype Operator">_≤</a> <a id="22336" class="Number">2</a><a id="22337" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22339" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="22341" class="Number">0</a> <a id="22343" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22345" class="Number">1</a> <a id="22347" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22349" class="Number">2</a> <a id="22351" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2881" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="22353" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="22355" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22357" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a> <a id="22361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="22363" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="22367" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a> <a id="22371" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="22373" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="22377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22378" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="22382" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a><a id="22385" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22387" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="22389" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21587" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Here `_∷_` and `[]` are the constructors of `All P` rather than of `List A`.
The three items are proofs of `0 ≤ 2`, `1 ≤ 2`, and `2 ≤ 2`, respectively.

(One might wonder whether a pattern such as `[_,_,_]` can be used to
construct values of type `All` as well as type `List`, since both use
the same constructors. Indeed it can, so long as both types are in
scope when the pattern is declared.  That's not the case here, since
`List` is defined before `[_,_,_]`, but `All` is defined later.)


## Any

Predicate `Any P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by some element of a list:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="22984" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Any"></a><a id="22989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22989" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22994" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22996" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22998" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23001" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23003" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23004" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23004" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23006" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23008" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23010" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23012" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23017" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23019" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="23024" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23026" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23028" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="23032" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Any.here"></a><a id="23040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a>  <a id="23046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23048" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23050" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23051" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23051" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23055" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23056" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23058" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23059" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23059" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23062" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23064" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="23069" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23070" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23072" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23074" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23004" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23076" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23051" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23080" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22989" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="23084" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23004" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23086" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23087" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23051" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23089" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="23091" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23059" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="23093" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="Any.there"></a><a id="23097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="23103" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23105" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23107" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23108" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23108" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23112" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23113" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23115" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23116" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23116" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23119" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23121" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="23126" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22994" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23127" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23129" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23131" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22989" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="23135" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23004" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23137" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23116" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23140" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23142" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22989" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="23146" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23004" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23148" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23149" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23108" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23151" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="23153" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23116" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="23155" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The first constructor provides evidence that the head of the list
satisfies `P`, while the second provides evidence that some element of
the tail of the list satisfies `P`.  For example, we can define list
membership as follows:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="23394" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="23400" class="Number">4</a> <a id="23402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23411" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="23406" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23481" class="Function Operator">_∉_</a>

<a id="_∈_"></a><a id="23411" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23411" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="23415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23417" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23419" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23420" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23420" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23424" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23427" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23430" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23430" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23434" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23420" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23435" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23437" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23438" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23438" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23441" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23443" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="23448" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23420" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23449" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23451" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23453" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="23457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23457" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23459" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23411" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23461" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23461" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23464" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23466" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#22989" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="23470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23471" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23457" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23473" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡_</a><a id="23475" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23477" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23461" class="Bound">xs</a>

<a id="_∉_"></a><a id="23481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23481" class="Function Operator">_∉_</a> <a id="23485" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23487" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23489" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23490" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23490" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23492" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23494" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23497" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23500" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23500" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23502" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23504" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23490" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23505" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23508" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23508" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23511" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23513" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="23518" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23490" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23519" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23521" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23523" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="23527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23529" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23481" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="23531" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23531" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="23534" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23536" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="23538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23539" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23541" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23411" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23543" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23531" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="23545" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}For example, zero is an element of the list `[ 0 , 1 , 0 , 2 ]`.  Indeed, we can demonstrate
this fact in two different ways, corresponding to the two different
occurrences of zero in the list, as the first element and as the third element:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="23796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23796" class="Function">_</a> <a id="23798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23800" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23802" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23411" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23804" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="23806" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23808" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23810" class="Number">1</a> <a id="23812" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23814" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23816" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23818" class="Number">2</a> <a id="23820" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="23822" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="23824" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="23831" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

<a id="23837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23837" class="Function">_</a> <a id="23839" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23841" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23843" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23411" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23845" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="23847" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23849" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23851" class="Number">1</a> <a id="23853" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23855" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23857" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23859" class="Number">2</a> <a id="23861" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="23863" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="23865" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="23873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23874" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="23880" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23881" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="23886" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="23890" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Further, we can demonstrate that three is not in the list, because
any possible proof that it is in the list leads to contradiction:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="not-in"></a><a id="24034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24043" class="Number">3</a> <a id="24045" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23481" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="24047" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="24049" class="Number">0</a> <a id="24051" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24053" class="Number">1</a> <a id="24055" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24057" class="Number">0</a> <a id="24059" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24061" class="Number">2</a> <a id="24063" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="24065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24072" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24073" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="24078" class="Symbol">())</a>
<a id="24082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24089" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24090" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24096" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24097" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="24102" class="Symbol">()))</a>
<a id="24107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24114" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24115" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24121" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24122" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24129" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="24134" class="Symbol">())))</a>
<a id="24140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24148" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24155" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24161" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24162" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24168" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24169" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23040" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="24174" class="Symbol">()))))</a>
<a id="24181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="24188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24189" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24195" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24196" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24202" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24203" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24210" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#23097" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="24216" class="Symbol">()))))</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The five occurrences of `()` attest to the fact that there is no
possible evidence for `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 1`, `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 2`, and
`3 ∈ []`, respectively.

## All and append

A predicate holds for every element of one list appended to another if and
only if it holds for every element of both lists:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="All-++-⇔"></a><a id="24527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24527" class="Function">All-++-⇔</a> <a id="24536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24538" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24540" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24541" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24541" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24543" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24545" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24548" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24551" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24555" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24541" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24557" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24559" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24562" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24565" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24565" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24568" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24568" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="24571" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24573" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="24578" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24541" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24579" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24581" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="24585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="24589" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24592" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24565" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24595" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#3467" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="24598" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24568" class="Bound">ys</a><a id="24600" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#11947" class="Record Operator">⇔</a> <a id="24604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24605" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="24609" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24611" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24565" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24614" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24616" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="24620" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24551" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24622" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24568" class="Bound">ys</a><a id="24624" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="24626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24527" class="Function">All-++-⇔</a> <a id="24635" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24635" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24638" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24638" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="24641" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="24645" class="Keyword">record</a>
    <a id="24656" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="24658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#11987" class="Field">to</a>       <a id="24667" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24725" class="Function">to</a> <a id="24673" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24635" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24676" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24638" class="Bound">ys</a>
    <a id="24683" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="24685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#12004" class="Field">from</a>     <a id="24694" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="24697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24950" class="Function">from</a> <a id="24702" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24635" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24705" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24638" class="Bound">ys</a>
    <a id="24712" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="24716" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#24725" class="Function">to</a> <a id="24728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24730" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24732" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24733" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24733" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24735" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24737" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24740" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24742" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24743" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24743" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24745" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24747" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24733" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24749" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24751" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24754" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24757" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24757" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="24760" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24760" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="24763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24765" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="24770" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#24733" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24771" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24773" class="Symbol">→</a>

#### Exercise `Any-++-⇔` (recommended)

Prove a result similar to `All-++-⇔`, but with `Any` in place of `All`, and a suitable
replacement for `_×_`.  As a consequence, demonstrate an equivalence relating
`_∈_` and `_++_`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="25382" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `All-++-≃` (stretch)

Show that the equivalence `All-++-⇔` can be extended to an isomorphism.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="25523" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `¬Any≃All¬` (recommended)

Show that `Any` and `All` satisfy a version of De Morgan's Law:

    (¬_ ∘ Any P) xs ≃ All (¬_ ∘ P) xs

(Can you see why it is important that here `_∘_` is generalised
to arbitrary levels, as described in the section on
[universe polymorphism]({{ site.baseurl }}/Equality/#unipoly)?)

Do we also have the following?

    (¬_ ∘ All P) xs ≃ Any (¬_ ∘ P) xs

If so, prove; if not, explain why.


#### Exercise `All-∀` (practice)

Show that `All P xs` is isomorphic to `∀ {x} → x ∈ xs → P x`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="26086" class="Comment">-- You code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

#### Exercise `Any-∃` (practice)

Show that `Any P xs` is isomorphic to `∃[ x ] (x ∈ xs × P x)`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="26216" class="Comment">-- You code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

## Decidability of All

If we consider a predicate as a function that yields a boolean,
it is easy to define an analogue of `All`, which returns true if
a given predicate returns true for every element of a list:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="all"></a><a id="26461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26461" class="Function">all</a> <a id="26465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26467" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26470" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#26470" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26474" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26477" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26479" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26482" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#26470" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26486" href="Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#135" class="Datatype">Bool</a><a id="26490" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26494" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1067" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="26499" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#26470" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26501" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26503" href="Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#135" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="26508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26461" class="Function">all</a> <a id="26512" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#26512" class="Bound">p</a>  <a id="26515" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="26518" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#15293" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="26524" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Bool.Base.html#1015" class="Function Operator">_∧_</a> <a id="26528" href="Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#160" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a> <a id="26533" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="26535" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#12867" class="Function">map</a> <a id="26539" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#26512" class="Bound">p</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The function can be written in a particularly compact style by
using the higher-order functions `map` and `foldr`.

As one would hope, if we replace booleans by decidables there is again
an analogue of `All`.  First, return to the notion of a predicate `P` as
a function of type `A → Set`, taking a value `x` of type `A` into evidence
`P x` that a property holds for `x`.  Say that a predicate `P` is _decidable_
if we have a function that for a given `x` can decide `P x`:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Decidable"></a><a id="27023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27023" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27033" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27035" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27037" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27038" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27038" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27040" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27042" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="27045" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27047" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27049" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27050" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27038" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27052" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27054" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="27057" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27059" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27061" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="27065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27023" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27075" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27076" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27076" class="Bound">A</a><a id="27077" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27079" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27079" class="Bound">P</a>  <a id="27082" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27085" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27088" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27088" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27090" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27092" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27076" class="Bound">A</a><a id="27093" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27095" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27097" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#605" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="27101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27102" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27079" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="27104" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27088" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27105" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Then if predicate `P` is decidable, it is also decidable whether every
element of a list satisfies the predicate:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="All?"></a><a id="27229" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27229" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27236" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27238" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27239" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27239" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27243" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="27246" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27248" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27249" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27249" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="27251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27253" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27239" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27255" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27257" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="27260" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27264" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27023" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27274" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27249" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="27276" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27278" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27023" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27288" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27289" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21536" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="27293" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27249" class="Bound">P</a><a id="27294" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27296" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27229" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27301" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27301" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27304" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1096" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>                                 <a id="27339" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27342" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27346" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21587" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
<a id="27349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27229" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27354" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27354" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27358" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27358" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27360" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#1111" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27362" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27362" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="27364" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27366" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="27371" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27354" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27374" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27358" class="Bound">x</a>   <a id="27378" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27380" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27229" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27385" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27354" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27388" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27362" class="Bound">xs</a>
<a id="27391" class="Symbol">...</a>                 <a id="27411" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27413" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27417" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27420" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27422" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27426" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27426" class="Bound">Pxs</a>     <a id="27434" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27437" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27442" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27417" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27445" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27447" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27426" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27450" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27452" class="Symbol">...</a>                 <a id="27472" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27474" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27477" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27477" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="27481" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27483" class="Symbol">_</a>           <a id="27495" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27498" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27501" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="27504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27505" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27505" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27508" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27510" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27510" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27513" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27517" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27477" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="27521" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27505" class="Bound">Px</a>   <a id="27526" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="27528" class="CatchallClause Symbol">...</a><a id="27531" class="CatchallClause">                 </a><a id="27548" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="27549" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27550" class="CatchallClause Symbol">_</a><a id="27551" class="CatchallClause">      </a><a id="27557" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="27558" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27559" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="CatchallClause InductiveConstructor">no</a><a id="27561" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27562" class="CatchallClause Bound">¬Pxs</a>     <a id="27571" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27574" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27577" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="27580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27581" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27581" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27584" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#21604" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27586" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27586" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27589" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27591" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27593" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27562" class="Bound">¬Pxs</a> <a id="27598" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#27586" class="Bound">Pxs</a> <a id="27602" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}If the list is empty, then trivially `P` holds for every element of
the list.  Otherwise, the structure of the proof is similar to that
showing that the conjunction of two decidable propositions is itself
decidable, using `_∷_` rather than `⟨_,_⟩` to combine the evidence for
the head and tail of the list.


#### Exercise `any?` (stretch)

Just as `All` has analogues `all` and `All?` which determine whether a
predicate holds for every element of a list, so does `Any` have
analogues `any` and `Any?` which determine whether a predicate holds
for some element of a list.  Give their definitions.

</pre>{% endraw %}

#### Exercise `split` (stretch)

The relation `merge` holds when two lists merge to give a third list.

For example,
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="28707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28707" class="Function">_</a> <a id="28709" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28711" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#28352" class="Datatype">merge</a> <a id="28717" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="28719" class="Number">1</a> <a id="28721" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28723" class="Number">4</a> <a id="28725" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="28727" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="28729" class="Number">2</a> <a id="28731" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28733" class="Number">3</a> <a id="28735" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2850" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="28737" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="28739" class="Number">1</a> <a id="28741" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28743" class="Number">2</a> <a id="28745" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28747" class="Number">3</a> <a id="28749" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28751" class="Number">4</a> <a id="28753" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#2920" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="28755" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="28757" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part1/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="InductiveConstructor">left-∷</a> <a id="28766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28767" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#28569" class="InductiveConstructor">right-∷</a> <a id="28775" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28776" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#28569" class="InductiveConstructor">right-∷</a> <a id="28784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28785" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#28455" class="InductiveConstructor">left-∷</a> <a id="28792" href="plfa.part1.Lists.html#28405" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a><a id="28794" class="Symbol">)))</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
Given a decidable predicate and a list, we can split the list
into two lists that merge to give the original list, where all
elements of one list satisfy the predicate, and all elements of
the other do not satisfy the predicate.

Define the following variant of the traditional `filter` function on lists,
which given a decidable predicate and a list returns all elements of the
list satisfying the predicate:

    split : ∀ {A : Set} {P : A → Set} (P? : Decidable P) (xs : List A)
      → ∃[ ys ] ∃[ zs ] ( merge xs ys zs × All P ys × All (¬_ ∘ P) zs )

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="29363" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

<a id="29894" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="29901" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Unary.html" class="Module">Relation.Unary</a> <a id="29916" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="29922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29923" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Unary.html#3474" class="Function">Decidable</a><a id="29932" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="29934" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="29941" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.html" class="Module">Relation.Binary</a> <a id="29957" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="29963" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29964" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.Core.html#5557" class="Function">Decidable</a><a id="29973" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The standard library version of `IsMonoid` differs from the
one given here, in that it is also parameterised on an equivalence relation.

Both `Relation.Unary` and `Relation.Binary` define a version of `Decidable`,
one for unary relations (as used in this chapter where `P` ranges over
unary predicates) and one for binary relations (as used earlier, where `_≤_`
ranges over a binary relation).

## Unicode

This chapter uses the following unicode:

    ∷  U+2237  PROPORTION  (\::)
    ⊗  U+2297  CIRCLED TIMES  (\otimes, \ox)
    ∈  U+2208  ELEMENT OF  (\in)
    ∉  U+2209  NOT AN ELEMENT OF  (\inn, \notin)
